27.[Yoix] [C]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Yoix,http://dbpedia.org/resource/C_%28programming_language%29]
[o] Pointers and pointer arithmetic in the Yoix language is syntactically similar to what is found in the C language , but the Yoix implementation prevents using a pointer outside its bounds .


28.[Impulse C] [C]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Impulse_C,http://dbpedia.org/resource/C_%28programming_language%29]
[o] Impulse C development tools .


29.[Perl] [AWK]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Perl,http://dbpedia.org/resource/AWK]
[o] GNU Sed and Awk are used instead of Perl .


30.[William Makepeace Thackeray] [Henry Fielding]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/William_Makepeace_Thackeray,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Henry_Fielding]
[o] His proficiency in the two languages led him to translate into Dutch several of the works of Charles Dickens , William Makepeace Thackeray and others , and afterwards also of Henry Fielding , Laurence Sterne and Walter Scott .

2.[Coipasa Lake] [Lauca River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Coipasa_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Lauca_River]
[o] With a surface of 6 km ² , the Cotacotani holds a volume of water between 30 to 40 million of m ³ , which empty through Lauca River into Coipasa Lake , in Bolivia .


3.[Great Salt Lake] [Bear River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Great_Salt_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Bear_River_%28Utah%29]
[o] The Bear River today runs to the north and west of Grace and terminates in the Great Salt Lake .


4.[El Golfete] [Dulce River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/El_Golfete,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Dulce_River]
[o] The park covers an area of 130 km2 along the banks of the Dulce river and the El Golfete .

7.[Longcanoe Lake] [Whitesand River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Longcanoe_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Whitesand_River_%28Hewitson_River%29]

8.[Lake Houston] [San Jacinto River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Lake_Houston,http://dbpedia.org/resource/San_Jacinto_River_%28Texas%29]

9.[Hebgen Lake] [Madison River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Hebgen_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Madison_River]
[o] Spawning runs of large Brown trout into the Madison River in the Fall from Hebgen Lake outside the park attract a large number of anglers .


10.[Lake Murten] [Broye]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Lake_Murten,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Broye]

11.[Lake Bohinj] [Sava Bohinjka]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Lake_Bohinj,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Sava_Bohinjka]

12.[North Whitesand Lake] [Whitesand River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/North_Whitesand_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Whitesand_River_%28Hewitson_River%29]

24.[Maynard Lake] [English River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Maynard_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/English_River]

25.[Kaunas Reservoir] [Neman River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Kaunas_Reservoir,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Neman_River]
[o] Kaunas Reservoir -LRB- Kauno marios -RRB- is the largest Lithuanian artificial lake , created in 1959 by damming the Neman River near Kaunas and Rumšiškės .


26.[Duck Lake] [Upper Mississippi River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Duck_Lake_%28Iowa%29,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Upper_Mississippi_River]
[o] Duck Lake is a small lake in the wetlands on the western shore of the Upper Mississippi River , just north of Lansing , Iowa , in northeastern Allamakee County .


27.[Richard B. Russell Lake] [Savannah River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Richard_B._Russell_Lake,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Savannah_River]

29.[Apache Lake] [Salt River]		[http://dbpedia.org/resource/Apache_Lake_%28Arizona%29,http://dbpedia.org/resource/Salt_River_%28Arizona%29]
